 Born on the 23rd of January, 1960, in the working family of Nagina, a small town in Mewat district, Haryana, the narrator Bhagwandas Morwal distinguished himself in Hindi fiction from his works of deep narrative exploration, research and works keeping the untouchable themes at the center
 Have been made unke vishay anuthe or paatr lokjeevi hai
 The range of his writing is so amazing that don't ask
 isiilie pathakon ko unki likhi kitabon ke prati bahut utsukata rahati he
 Whether it was a black mountain novel written on the backdrop of Mewat or sand, a novel written in the center of a caste group called Jarayampesha, readers appreciated his works
 enjio samskruti kii padtaal karte unke upanyaas ‘narak maseehaa’ ko bhi khub vaahvahee mili, to dharm kii aad main stri-shoshan ko centre main rakhkar likhe gaye ‘halaala’ par khub naatak khele ja rahe hai
 His latest novel came a year ago, but the readers keep searching for 'sur Banjaran' written with a gimmick of Hathras style in the center
 unke lekhan par kai shodh ho chuke hai
 Today, discussion on contemporary fiction is incomplete without Bhagwandas Morwal threatening his writings against cultural supremacy
 sahitya ajtak ne un ke janmdin par unase lambii baatcheet kii
 Part Exclusive How and when did you become a writer? Bhagwandas Morwal: Becoming a writer is not such a process that you become a writer overnight
 yah ek lambii prakriya he jo aapke sanchit anubhavon kaa nirmaan he
 Secondly, after all, who do we call writers? Whatever you write him? If it is necessary to become a writer then it is difficult to tell when and how i became a writer
 lekhak hona meri nazar main vah he jab aapke likhe kaa pathak intazaar karte hon
 In this way, i became a writer when i started to mold my early experiences into stories and poems and it started in the late 1980s
 lekin ham lekhak kisi ko tab maanate hai jab uski koi pustak na aa jaae
 My first book, which was the essence of these raw-hearted experiences, was published in 1986 under the title Stila Man Kahani Collection
 pehali kitaab chhapane main kitna vakt laga, kya-kya dikkatein jhelni padin?bhagavaandas morwal:mujhe is sangrah ko prakashit karaane main kisi bhi tarah kii pareshaani kaa saamana nahin karnaa padaa
 Often we see that some people pay money to the publisher in the name of financial support for their first book, at least i did not give it then
 aisa nahin he ki yah parampara us samay nahin thi, yah parampara to tab se he jab se prakaashan vyavsaay shuru hua tha
 Yes, a funny story with my first book was that the publisher also printed a few articles with stories from the files i had given him to complete the book
 mevaat or vahaan kaa jivan aapke lekhan ke centre main rahaa he
 Even it has been twenty years since the black mountain was printed, has there been any change in the life there since then? How much has changed in Mewat? Bhagwandas Morwal: It is true that this is the twentieth year of publication of Kala Pahar
 1999 ke lagbhag ant main yah upanyaas raajakmal prakaashan samooh ke radhakrishna prakaashan se prakashit hua tha
 This was my first novel and to be honest, this novel gave me the authorial acceptance that you have mentioned in your first question
 kehane ko ham kaala pahaad ko aaj se bees saal pehle kaa mevaat kah sakate hai lekin sachai yah he ki isamen sirf bees varsh pehle kaa mevaat nahin he, balki ek puri sadi kaa mevaat he
 In which it has a golden past, Mewat also has a glorious history
 isamen mevaat kii mishrit samskruti kaa pakkaa or gadha rang dekha ja saktaa he to tezi se is rang ke fike padane kii pidaa bhi aap mahasoos kar sakate hai
 You have asked about the change in the life of Mewat by quoting this novel
 main yahaan yah kahana chahta hum ki in pichley do dashakon main sirf mevaat hi nahin balki hamaare puure bhartiya samaaj main badlaav aayaa he
 Especially after the Ram janmabhoomi-babri Masjid dispute, mutual trust in our society has decreased
 ek tarah se mevaat ko ham badalte gramin bharat ke rup main dekh sakate hai
 i can say that religious fundamentalism has increased in all religions and communities alike
 aapaki nazar main aapaki sabase acchhee kriti koun si he or kyon?bhagavaandas morwal:is sawaal kaa jawaab dena kisi bhi lekhak ke liye sabase mushkil kaam he
 He likes every piece of his work
 haa, koi-koi kriti ek lekhak kii pahchaan ban jaati he
